the American experimental rock band, will be at Zorlu PSM on May 16th!   Considered a part of the no wave movement which started in the 70s and lifted its effectiveneess in the 80s, Swans was led by singer/songwriter Michael Gira. The band was active between 1982 and 1997, with Jarboe (keyboards, vocal, songwriter) and Norman Westberg (guitar) being the other two permanent members. The name of the band was explained by Gira as swans having ugly temperaments  yet being majestic and beautiful looking creatures.  Swans is compared to Joy Division with their post-punk sounds, although it adds influences of blues and jazz in the mix. The lyrics of Gira, on the other hand, are influenced by Jean Genet and Marquis de Sade. Having released its debut album Filth in 1983, Swans went on to release 9 more until it disbanded in 1998.  Michael Gira continued his musical career with Angels of Light after Swans disbanded and explains that he decided to return with Swans while he was playing The Provider on stage one day, claiming he felt \"a nascent urge right then to re-form or reinvigorate Swans because I remembered how elevating and intense that experience was\". Having released the solo album titled I Am Not Insane in order to collect funding for the upcoming Swans album, Gira is carrying his works without Jarboe since 2010.  After getting back together, Swans released My Father Will Guide Me Up a Rope to the Sky in 2010. The Best Albums of the Decade (2010-2014) of the renowned music website Pitchfork featured two albums of Swans; The Seer (2012) and To Be Kind (2014). Swans released its 14th album The Glowing Man in 2016 on the Young God Records and Mute Records label.   On May 16th, Zorlu PSM will host Swans, the American band which features a no wave influenced experimental post-punk
